# HeroForge Anew 3.5 v7.4.1.2-a1 — Named Cell Index

Reference for locating data in the ODS spreadsheet.
Source: HeroForge Anew 3.5 v7.4.1.2-a1.ods

## Summary

- **Sheets:** 64
- **Named ranges/cells:** 7970
- **Named expressions:** 71
- **Print areas:** 9
